# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-loki` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/grafana-loki$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

---

**Sourcegraph Repositories:** `github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec`, `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-loki`, `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir`

# Grafana Dashboard Schema Version Migration Pipeline

## Your Task

Find all Go and TypeScript source files in grafana/grafana that implement the dashboard JSON schema version migration pipeline. Identify: the migration runner (apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/), the versioned migration function registry (GetMigrations returning version-to-function map), individual migration steps (e.g. V2, V36), and the frontend DashboardMigrator in TypeScript that mirrors the backend logic.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` (grafana/grafana)
- `sg-evals/grafana-loki` (grafana/loki)
- `sg-evals/grafana-mimir` (grafana/mimir)

Transforms legacy JSON dashboards to migrated JSON format\\n47: - Handles backward compatibility for older dashboard formats\\n48: - See [SchemaVersion Migration Guide](./schemaversion/README.md) for detailed instructions on creating new schema migrations\\n49: \\n50: #### v1 to v2 Conversion:\\n51: - API version conversions between different Kubernetes API versions\\n52: - Transforms JSON dashboards to structured dashboard format\\n53: - v2 schema is the stable, typed schema with proper type definitions\\n54: - Handles modern dashboard features and Kubernetes-native storage\\n55: \\n56: ## Conversion Matrix\\n57: \\n58: The system supports conversions between all dashboard API versions:\\n59: \\n60: | From \u2193 / To \u2192 | v0alpha1 | v1beta1 | v2alpha1 | v2beta1 |\\n61: |---------------|----------|---------|----------|---------|\\n62: | **v0alpha1**  | \u2713        | \u2713       | \u2713        | \u2713       |\\n63: | **v1beta1**   | \u2713        | \u2713       | \u2713        | \u2713       |\\n64: | **v2alpha1**  | \u2713        | \u2713       | \u2713        | \u2713       |\\n65: | **v2beta1**   | \u2713        | \u2713       | \u2713        | \u2713       |\\n66: \\n67: Each conversion path is automatically instrumented with metrics and logging.\\n68: \\n69: ## API Versions\\n70: \\n71: The supported dashboard API versions are:\\n72: \\n73: - `dashboard.grafana.app/v0alpha1` - Legacy JSON dashboard format\\n74: - `dashboard.grafana.app/v1beta1` - Migrated JSON dashboard format  \\n75: - `dashboard.grafana.app/v2alpha1` - New structured dashboard format\\n76: - `dashboard.grafana.app/v2beta1` - Enhanced structured dashboard format\\n77: \\n78: ## Schema Versions\\n79: \\n80: Schema versions (v13-v42) apply only to v0alpha1 and v1beta1 dashboards:\\n81: \\n82: - implements a comprehensive dashboard JSON schema version migration system spanning both backend (Go) and frontend (TypeScript) components. The pipeline consists of 41 sequential schema migrations (v2 through v42) that transform legacy dashboards to the current schema while maintaining backward compatibility.\\n\\n### Backend Migration System (apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/)\\n\\n#### Migration Runner\\nThe core migration orchestrator is implemented in `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/migrate.go`. The `Initialize()` function sets up a singleton migrator instance that holds the complete version-to-function mapping. The `Migrate()` function executes sequential migrations on a dashboard object, tracking schema version progression from the input version to a target version (default: v42).\\n\\nThe migrator performs the following operations in sequence:\\n1. Cleans up backend-specific properties not present in frontend saves\\n2. Tracks original transformations and field configs for property preservation\\n3. Applies frontend defaults to replicate frontend initialization behavior\\n4. Ensures all panels have unique IDs\\n5. Executes versioned migrations sequentially\\n6. Adds built-in annotation query\\n7. Cleans up dashboard properties for save compatibility\\n\\n#### Versioned Migration Registry\\nThe migration registry is centralized in `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migrations.go`. The `GetMigrations()` function returns a map[int]SchemaVersionMigrationFunc where each version number maps to a migration function. This registry implements a factory pattern that binds data source providers to migrations that require them (V33 and V36). The schema version range spans from v2 through v42 (minimum supported is v13, latest is v42).\\n\\nThe registry uses the type `SchemaVersionMigrationFunc` defined as: `func(context.Context, map[string]interface{}) error`. Most migrations are simple stateless functions, while V33 and V36 return closures that capture the DataSourceInfoProvider for datasource resolution.\\n\\n#### Individual Migration Steps\\nAll individual migration implementations follow the pattern of versioned Go files (v2.go through v42.go) in the schemaversion package. Key migrations include:\\n\\n- **V2**: Migrates legacy services.filter structure to top-level templating and time properties\\n- **V6**: Moves drop-downs to new annotation schema and converts template variables from 'filter' type to 'query'\\n- **V7**: Migrates nav structure to timepicker\\n- **V16**: Performs grid layout migration from row-based to grid-based layout system (major structural change)\\n- **V23**: Updates template variable handling\\n- **V24**: Migrates table panels with timeseries-to-rows transformations\\n- **V31**: Handles labels-to-fields transformer migration\\n- **V33**: Migrates datasource references with DataSourceInfoProvider lookup\\n- **V36**: Transforms datasource references from string format to structured UID-based objects with type and apiVersion\\n- **V38**: Migrates table cell options and display modes\\n- **V40**: Ensures refresh property is string type\\n- **V41-V42**: Final schema evolution steps\\n\\n#### Support Infrastructure\\n`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migration_utils.go` provides utility functions for type-safe data access: `GetStringValue()`, `GetBoolValue()`, `GetIntValue()`, `GetFloatValue()`, and type conversion functions. These utilities mirror frontend type coercion behavior.\\n\\n`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/datasource_utils.go` handles datasource reference resolution, converting datasource names to UID-based DataSourceRef objects.\\n\\n`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/errors.go` defines `MigrationError` and `MinimumVersionError` types for structured error reporting.\\n\\n`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/frontend_defaults.go` replicates frontend DashboardModel and PanelModel default initialization behavior, ensuring backend migrations apply the same defaults the frontend would apply during model construction.\\n\\n`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/metrics.go` instruments migrations with Prometheus metrics for observability.\\n\\n### Frontend Migration System (public/app/features/dashboard/state/)\\n\\n#### DashboardMigrator TypeScript Class\\nThe frontend implementation mirrors backend logic in `public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardMigrator.ts`. The class exports `DASHBOARD_SCHEMA_VERSION = 42` as the target version and implements the `updateSchema()` method. This method contains conditional migration blocks that execute based on version ranges (e.g., `if (oldVersion < 16 && finalTargetVersion >= 16)`), allowing targeted migrations that skip intermediate versions when a dashboard is already at a higher version.\\n\\nThe TypeScript implementation handles:\\n- Legacy services.filter migration (v2)\\n- Pulldown/annotation structure migration (v6)\\n- Timepicker migration from nav (v7)\\n- InfluxDB query schema migrations (v8)\\n- Row-to-grid layout migration (v16) with complex panel dimension calculations\\n- Template variable migrations (v23, v27)\\n- Table panel migrations (v24)\\n- Datasource reference transformations (v33, v36)\\n- Panel type auto-migrations for deprecated types\\n\\n#### Integration with DashboardModel\\nThe `public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardModel.ts` constructor integrates schema migration by calling `updateSchema()` during initialization. The DashboardModel accepts a `targetSchemaVersion` option to support single-version migrations for testing, defaulting to the latest `DASHBOARD_SCHEMA_VERSION`.\\n\\n### Testing and Validation\\n\\n#### Backend Tests\\nTest files exist for each migration step (v2_test.go through v42_test.go) in the schemaversion package, validating individual migration behavior with JSON fixtures.\\n\\n#### Frontend Tests\\nMultiple test files validate frontend migration consistency:\\n- `DashboardMigrator.test.ts`: Unit tests for individual schema migration logic\\n- `DashboardMigratorToBackend.test.ts`: Comparison tests that verify backend and frontend migrations produce identical results by running curated test dashboards through both pipelines\\n- `DashboardMigratorSingleVersion.test.ts`: Tests single-version migrations (e.g., v15\u2192v16)\\n- `DashboardMigratorToBackend.devDashboards.test.ts`: Tests dev dashboard migrations with full datasource resolution\\n\\nThese tests ensure consistency between frontend and backend migration logic, using test data fixtures in `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/testdata/input/` and comparing outputs against expected results in `testdata/output/`.\\n\\n### Migration Execution Flow\\n\\n1. **Backend Path**: Dashboard JSON \u2192 Backend migration.Migrate() \u2192 Apply all schema migrations (v0-v42) \u2192 Output v42 JSON\\n2. **Frontend Path**: Dashboard JSON \u2192 DashboardModel constructor \u2192 DashboardMigrator.updateSchema() \u2192 Apply schema migrations \u2192 PanelModel creation \u2192 Output v42 dashboard object\\n\\nThe system maintains strict backward compatibility by supporting all historical schema versions and enforcing sequential migration execution. The minimum supported version is v13, while v42 is locked as the final version for the v1 dashboard API, with future enhancements directed to panel-level migrations and the v2 API version.\"\n}\n",
